TriggerInitObject.ExecuteText = (MxBigString) =' ******************************************************************************************************
' Template name : $GSK_UserDefined
' Script name   : TriggerInitObject
' ******************************************************************************************************
' Description 
'   This script Controls the activation of initializing

' ******************************************************************************************************
' History 
' 	v1.0	25/05/2009	GSK : Release
' ******************************************************************************************************

'Initilalize the pointer to MyAreaConnectionName
If not bInitializingTriggerInitObject then
	pMyArea_Initialized.BindTo("MyArea._Initialized");
	bInitializingTriggerInitObject = 1;
	iWaitingTime = -1;
	if me.Area == "" then
		bFirstAreaInitializing = 1;
	endif;	
endif;

'object is in initializing mode during the waiting time
'object is initialized after the waiting time
if (isgood(pMyArea_Initialized) and pMyArea_Initialized and (pMyArea_Initialized <> bPrevMyArea_Initialized)) or (me.InitializeObjectsRq) or (bFirstAreaInitializing) then
	iWaitingTime = iWaitingTime + 1;
	IF iWaitingTime >= me._InitScanCycles then
		bPrevMyArea_Initialized = pMyArea_Initialized;
		me._Initialized = 1;
		me._Initializing = 0;
		me.InitializeObjectsRq = 0;
		bFirstAreaInitializing = 0;
		iWaitingTime = 0;
	else
		me._Initialized = 0;
		me._Initializing = 1;
	endif;
else
	bPrevMyArea_Initialized = pMyArea_Initialized;
endif;

' Template name : $GSK_UserDefined

'
' ******************************************************************************************************
' History 
' 	v1.0	25/05/2009	GSK : Release
' ******************************************************************************************************

dim sConnectionName	as string;

'Initilalize the pointer to MyAreaConnectionName
If not bInitializingConnectionName then
	pMyAreaConnectionName.BindTo("MyArea.ConnectionName");
	bInitializingConnectionName = 1;
	iWaitingTime = -1;	
endif;

'Wait for a period of _InitScanCycles second before affect the connectionname
iWaitingTime = iWaitingTime + 1;
IF iWaitingTime >= me._InitScanCycles then

	'Copy the connectionName from OverrideconnectionName
	sPrev_OverrideConnectionName = me._OverrideConnectionName;
	sConnectionName = me._OverrideConnectionName;

	'Copy the ConnectionName from MyArea
	if isgood(pMyAreaConnectionName) then
		sPrevMyAreaConnectionName = pMyAreaConnectionName;
		if sConnectionName == "" then
			sConnectionName = pMyAreaConnectionName;
		endif;
	endif;

	'Assigne the me.ConnectionName
	me.ConnectionName = sConnectionName;
	
	iWaitingTime = 0;
endif;

'

' ******************************************************************************************************

dim sLanguage	as string;

'Initilalize the pointer to MyAreaLanguage
If not bInitializingLanguage then
	pMyAreaLanguage.BindTo("MyArea.Language");
	bInitializingLanguage = 1;
	iWaitingTime = -1;	
	if Me.Area == "" then	
		me.Language = me._DefaultLanguage;
	endif;
endif;

'Wait for a period of _InitScanCycles second before affect the language
iWaitingTime = iWaitingTime + 1;
IF iWaitingTime >= me._InitScanCycles then

	'Copy the language from OverrideLanguage
	sPrev_OverrideLanguage = me._OverrideLanguage;
	sLanguage = me._OverrideLanguage;

	'Copy the Language from MyArea
	if isgood(pMyAreaLanguage) then
		sPrevMyAreaLanguage = pMyAreaLanguage;
		if sLanguage == "" then
			sLanguage = pMyAreaLanguage;
		endif;
	endif;

	'Copy the DefaultLanguage
	if sLanguage == "" then
		sLanguage = me._DefaultLanguage;
	endif;

	'Assign the me.Language
	me.Language = sLanguage;
	
	iWaitingTime = 0;
endif;

Sx_InitObject.ExecuteText = (MxBigString) =' ******************************************************************************************************
' Template name : $TEC_CM_Analog_2A_Sx
' Script name   : Sx_InitObject
' ******************************************************************************************************
' Description 
'   This script is used to connect variables to PLC
'
' ******************************************************************************************************
' History 
' 	v1.0	19/05/2011	FAB : Release
' ******************************************************************************************************

IF iInitParam == 1 THEN
	DIM NotUsed as Float;

	NotUsed = Me.PV;

	iInitParam = 2;
ENDIF;

IF iInitParam == 0 THEN
	'Assign PLC sources
	'Non Boolean values
	IF Me.Simu == True THEN
		Me.PV.Input.InputSource = "Me.PV_Simu";
	ELSE
		Me.PV.Input.InputSource = Me.ConnectionName + "." + me.PLC_Adr;
	ENDIF;
	iInitParam = 1;
ENDIF;

IF iInitParam == 2 THEN
	iInitParam = 0;
ENDIF;

sPrevConnectionName = me.ConnectionName;
sPrevSimu = Me.Simu;

TriggerInitObject.ExecuteText = (MxBigString) =' ******************************************************************************************************
' Template name : $GSK_UserDefined
' Script name   : TriggerInitObject
' ******************************************************************************************************
' Description 
'   This script Controls the activation of initializing

' ******************************************************************************************************
' History 
' 	v1.0	25/05/2009	GSK : Release
' ******************************************************************************************************

'Initilalize the pointer to MyAreaConnectionName
If not bInitializingTriggerInitObject then
	pMyArea_Initialized.BindTo("MyArea._Initialized");
	bInitializingTriggerInitObject = 1;
	iWaitingTime = -1;
	if me.Area == "" then
		bFirstAreaInitializing = 1;
	endif;	
endif;

'object is in initializing mode during the waiting time
'object is initialized after the waiting time
if (isgood(pMyArea_Initialized) and pMyArea_Initialized and (pMyArea_Initialized <> bPrevMyArea_Initialized)) or (me.InitializeObjectsRq) or (bFirstAreaInitializing) then
	iWaitingTime = iWaitingTime + 1;
	IF iWaitingTime >= me._InitScanCycles then
		bPrevMyArea_Initialized = pMyArea_Initialized;
		me._Initialized = 1;
		me._Initializing = 0;
		me.InitializeObjectsRq = 0;
		bFirstAreaInitializing = 0;
		iWaitingTime = 0;
	else
		me._Initialized = 0;
		me._Initializing = 1;
	endif;
else
	bPrevMyArea_Initialized = pMyArea_Initialized;
endif;

	pMyAreaConnectionName.BindTo("MyArea.ConnectionName");
	bInitializingConnectionName = 1;
	iWaitingTime = -1;	
endif;

'Wait for a period of _InitScanCycles second before affect the connectionname
iWaitingTime = iWaitingTime + 1;
IF iWaitingTime >= me._InitScanCycles then

	'Copy the connectionName from OverrideconnectionName
	sPrev_OverrideConnectionName = me._OverrideConnectionName;
	sConnectionName = me._OverrideConnectionName;

	'Copy the ConnectionName from MyArea
	if isgood(pMyAreaConnectionName) then
		sPrevMyAreaConnectionName = pMyAreaConnectionName;
		if sConnectionName == "" then
			sConnectionName = pMyAreaConnectionName;
		endif;
	endif;

	'Assigne the me.ConnectionName
	me.ConnectionName = sConnectionName;
	
	iWaitingTime = 0;
endif;

'

' 	v1.0	19/05/2011	FAB : Release
' ******************************************************************************************************

IF iInitParam == 1 THEN
	DIM NotUsed as Float;

	NotUsed = Me.PV;

	iInitParam = 2;
ENDIF;

IF iInitParam == 0 THEN
	'Assign PLC sources
	'Non Boolean values
	IF Me.Simu == True THEN
		Me.PV.Input.InputSource = "Me.PV_Simu";
	ELSE
		Me.PV.Input.InputSource = Me.ConnectionName + "." + me.PLC_Adr;
	ENDIF;
	iInitParam = 1;
ENDIF;

IF iInitParam == 2 THEN
	iInitParam = 0;
ENDIF;

sPrevConnectionName = me.ConnectionName;
sPrevSimu = Me.Simu;

' ******************************************************************************************************

'Initilalize the pointer to MyAreaConnectionName
If not bInitializingTriggerInitObject then
	pMyArea_Initialized.BindTo("MyArea._Initialized");
	bInitializingTriggerInitObject = 1;
	iWaitingTime = -1;
	if me.Area == "" then
		bFirstAreaInitializing = 1;
	endif;	
endif;

'object is in initializing mode during the waiting time
'object is initialized after the waiting time
if (isgood(pMyArea_Initialized) and pMyArea_Initialized and (pMyArea_Initialized <> bPrevMyArea_Initialized)) or (me.InitializeObjectsRq) or (bFirstAreaInitializing) then
	iWaitingTime = iWaitingTime + 1;
	IF iWaitingTime >= me._InitScanCycles then
		bPrevMyArea_Initialized = pMyArea_Initialized;
		me._Initialized = 1;
		me._Initializing = 0;
		me.InitializeObjectsRq = 0;
		bFirstAreaInitializing = 0;
		iWaitingTime = 0;
	else
		me._Initialized = 0;
		me._Initializing = 1;
	endif;
else
	bPrevMyArea_Initialized = pMyArea_Initialized;
endif;

If not bInitializingConnectionName then
	pMyAreaConnectionName.BindTo("MyArea.ConnectionName");
	bInitializingConnectionName = 1;
	iWaitingTime = -1;	
endif;

'Wait for a period of _InitScanCycles second before affect the connectionname
iWaitingTime = iWaitingTime + 1;
IF iWaitingTime >= me._InitScanCycles then

	'Copy the connectionName from OverrideconnectionName
	sPrev_OverrideConnectionName = me._OverrideConnectionName;
	sConnectionName = me._OverrideConnectionName;

	'Copy the ConnectionName from MyArea
	if isgood(pMyAreaConnectionName) then
		sPrevMyAreaConnectionName = pMyAreaConnectionName;
		if sConnectionName == "" then
			sConnectionName = pMyAreaConnectionName;
		endif;
	endif;

	'Assigne the me.ConnectionName
	me.ConnectionName = sConnectionName;
	
	iWaitingTime = 0;

		me.Language = me._DefaultLanguage;
	endif;

		endif;

Sx_InitObject.ExecuteText = (MxBigString) =' ******************************************************************************************************
' Template name : $TEC_CM_Analog_2A_Sx
' Script name   : Sx_InitObject
' ******************************************************************************************************
' Description 
'   This script is used to connect variables to PLC
'
' ******************************************************************************************************
' History 
' 	v1.0	19/05/2011	FAB : Release
' ******************************************************************************************************

IF iInitParam == 1 THEN
	DIM NotUsed as Float;

	NotUsed = Me.PV;

	iInitParam = 2;
ENDIF;

IF iInitParam == 0 THEN
	'Assign PLC sources
	'Non Boolean values
	IF Me.Simu == True THEN
		Me.PV.Input.InputSource = "Me.PV_Simu";
	ELSE
		Me.PV.Input.InputSource = Me.ConnectionName + "." + me.PLC_Adr;
	ENDIF;
	iInitParam = 1;
ENDIF;

IF iInitParam == 2 THEN
	iInitParam = 0;
ENDIF;

sPrevConnectionName = me.ConnectionName;
sPrevSimu = Me.Simu;

TriggerInitObject._ExternalName = (MxString) =No Data
TriggerInitObject._InternalName = (MxString) =No Data
TriggerInitObject.ExecuteText = (MxBigString) =' ******************************************************************************************************
' Template name : $GSK_UserDefined
' Script name   : TriggerInitObject
' ******************************************************************************************************
' Description 
'   This script Controls the activation of initializing

' ******************************************************************************************************
' History 
' 	v1.0	25/05/2009	GSK : Release
' ******************************************************************************************************

'Initilalize the pointer to MyAreaConnectionName
If not bInitializingTriggerInitObject then
	pMyArea_Initialized.BindTo("MyArea._Initialized");
	bInitializingTriggerInitObject = 1;
	iWaitingTime = -1;
	if me.Area == "" then
		bFirstAreaInitializing = 1;
	endif;	
endif;

'object is in initializing mode during the waiting time
'object is initialized after the waiting time
if (isgood(pMyArea_Initialized) and pMyArea_Initialized and (pMyArea_Initialized <> bPrevMyArea_Initialized)) or (me.InitializeObjectsRq) or (bFirstAreaInitializing) then
	iWaitingTime = iWaitingTime + 1;
	IF iWaitingTime >= me._InitScanCycles then
		bPrevMyArea_Initialized = pMyArea_Initialized;
		me._Initialized = 1;
		me._Initializing = 0;
		me.InitializeObjectsRq = 0;
		bFirstAreaInitializing = 0;
		iWaitingTime = 0;
	else
		me._Initialized = 0;
		me._Initializing = 1;
	endif;
else
	bPrevMyArea_Initialized = pMyArea_Initialized;
endif;
TriggerInitObject._Binary = (MxQualifiedStruct) =0

SetConnectionName.ExecuteText = (MxBigString) =' ******************************************************************************************************
' Template name : $GSK_UserDefined

'   It will compose the me.ConnectionName
'
' ******************************************************************************************************
' History 
' 	v1.0	25/05/2009	GSK : Release
' ******************************************************************************************************

dim sConnectionName	as string;

'Initilalize the pointer to MyAreaConnectionName
If not bInitializingConnectionName then
	pMyAreaConnectionName.BindTo("MyArea.ConnectionName");
	bInitializingConnectionName = 1;
	iWaitingTime = -1;	
endif;

'Wait for a period of _InitScanCycles second before affect the connectionname
iWaitingTime = iWaitingTime + 1;
IF iWaitingTime >= me._InitScanCycles then

	'Copy the connectionName from OverrideconnectionName
	sPrev_OverrideConnectionName = me._OverrideConnectionName;
	sConnectionName = me._OverrideConnectionName;

	'Copy the ConnectionName from MyArea
	if isgood(pMyAreaConnectionName) then
		sPrevMyAreaConnectionName = pMyAreaConnectionName;
		if sConnectionName == "" then
			sConnectionName = pMyAreaConnectionName;
		endif;
	endif;

	'Assigne the me.ConnectionName
	me.ConnectionName = sConnectionName;
	
	iWaitingTime = 0;
endif;

'

' 	v1.0	25/05/2009	GSK : Release
' ******************************************************************************************************

dim sLanguage	as string;

'Initilalize the pointer to MyAreaLanguage
If not bInitializingLanguage then
	pMyAreaLanguage.BindTo("MyArea.Language");
	bInitializingLanguage = 1;
	iWaitingTime = -1;	
	if Me.Area == "" then	
		me.Language = me._DefaultLanguage;
	endif;
endif;

'Wait for a period of _InitScanCycles second before affect the language
iWaitingTime = iWaitingTime + 1;
IF iWaitingTime >= me._InitScanCycles then

	'Copy the language from OverrideLanguage
	sPrev_OverrideLanguage = me._OverrideLanguage;
	sLanguage = me._OverrideLanguage;

	'Copy the Language from MyArea
	if isgood(pMyAreaLanguage) then
		sPrevMyAreaLanguage = pMyAreaLanguage;
		if sLanguage == "" then
			sLanguage = pMyAreaLanguage;
		endif;
	endif;

	'Copy the DefaultLanguage
	if sLanguage == "" then
		sLanguage = me._DefaultLanguage;
	endif;

	'Assign the me.Language
	me.Language = sLanguage;
	
	iWaitingTime = 0;

	DIM NotUsed as Float;

	NotUsed = Me.PV;

	iInitParam = 2;

	'Assign PLC sources
	'Non Boolean values
	IF Me.Simu == True THEN
		Me.PV.Input.InputSource = "Me.PV_Simu";
	ELSE
		Me.PV.Input.InputSource = Me.ConnectionName + "." + me.PLC_Adr;
	ENDIF;
	iInitParam = 1;
ENDIF;

IF iInitParam == 2 THEN
	iInitParam = 0;
ENDIF;

sPrevSimu = Me.Simu;

TriggerInitObject._ExternalName = (MxString) =No Data
TriggerInitObject._InternalName = (MxString) =No Data
TriggerInitObject.ExecuteText = (MxBigString) =' ******************************************************************************************************
' Template name : $GSK_UserDefined
' Script name   : TriggerInitObject
' ******************************************************************************************************
' Description 
'   This script Controls the activation of initializing

' ******************************************************************************************************
' History 
' 	v1.0	25/05/2009	GSK : Release
' ******************************************************************************************************

'Initilalize the pointer to MyAreaConnectionName
If not bInitializingTriggerInitObject then
	pMyArea_Initialized.BindTo("MyArea._Initialized");
	bInitializingTriggerInitObject = 1;
	iWaitingTime = -1;
	if me.Area == "" then
		bFirstAreaInitializing = 1;
	endif;	
endif;

'object is in initializing mode during the waiting time
'object is initialized after the waiting time
if (isgood(pMyArea_Initialized) and pMyArea_Initialized and (pMyArea_Initialized <> bPrevMyArea_Initialized)) or (me.InitializeObjectsRq) or (bFirstAreaInitializing) then
	iWaitingTime = iWaitingTime + 1;
	IF iWaitingTime >= me._InitScanCycles then
		bPrevMyArea_Initialized = pMyArea_Initialized;
		me._Initialized = 1;
		me._Initializing = 0;
		me.InitializeObjectsRq = 0;
		bFirstAreaInitializing = 0;
		iWaitingTime = 0;
	else
		me._Initialized = 0;
		me._Initializing = 1;
	endif;
else
	bPrevMyArea_Initialized = pMyArea_Initialized;
endif;
TriggerInitObject._Binary = (MxQualifiedStruct) =0
TriggerInitObject.AliasReferences = (MxReferenceType) =No Data
TriggerInitObject.Aliases = (MxString) =No Data
TriggerInitObject._TriggerTypeEnum = (MxString) =WhileTrue,WhileFalse,OnTrue,OnFalse,DataChange,Periodic
TriggerInitObject.TriggerType = (MxQualifiedEnum) =WhileTrue
TriggerInitObject.Expression = (MxBigString) =(not bInitializingTriggerInitObject) or (isgood(pMyArea_Initialized) and (pMyArea_Initialized <> bPrevMyArea_Initialized)) or (me.InitializeObjectsRq) or (bFirstAreaInitializing)
TriggerInitObject.DataChangeDeadband = (MxDouble) =0,0

'
' ******************************************************************************************************
' History 
' 	v1.0	25/05/2009	GSK : Release
' ******************************************************************************************************

dim sConnectionName	as string;

'Initilalize the pointer to MyAreaConnectionName
If not bInitializingConnectionName then
	pMyAreaConnectionName.BindTo("MyArea.ConnectionName");
	bInitializingConnectionName = 1;
	iWaitingTime = -1;	
endif;

'Wait for a period of _InitScanCycles second before affect the connectionname
iWaitingTime = iWaitingTime + 1;
IF iWaitingTime >= me._InitScanCycles then

	'Copy the connectionName from OverrideconnectionName
	sPrev_OverrideConnectionName = me._OverrideConnectionName;
	sConnectionName = me._OverrideConnectionName;

	'Copy the ConnectionName from MyArea
	if isgood(pMyAreaConnectionName) then
		sPrevMyAreaConnectionName = pMyAreaConnectionName;
		if sConnectionName == "" then
			sConnectionName = pMyAreaConnectionName;
		endif;
	endif;

	'Assigne the me.ConnectionName
	me.ConnectionName = sConnectionName;
	
	iWaitingTime = 0;
endif;

	pMyAreaLanguage.BindTo("MyArea.Language");
	bInitializingLanguage = 1;
	iWaitingTime = -1;	
	if Me.Area == "" then	
		me.Language = me._DefaultLanguage;
	endif;
endif;

IF iWaitingTime >= me._InitScanCycles then

	'Copy the language from OverrideLanguage
	sPrev_OverrideLanguage = me._OverrideLanguage;
	sLanguage = me._OverrideLanguage;

	'Copy the Language from MyArea

		sPrevMyAreaLanguage = pMyAreaLanguage;
		if sLanguage == "" then
			sLanguage = pMyAreaLanguage;
		endif;
	endif;

	'Copy the DefaultLanguage

		sLanguage = me._DefaultLanguage;

	iWaitingTime = 0;

	'Assign PLC sources
	'Non Boolean values

		Me.PV.Input.InputSource = "Me.PV_Simu";
	ELSE
		Me.PV.Input.InputSource = Me.ConnectionName + "." + me.PLC_Adr;
	ENDIF;
	iInitParam = 1;
ENDIF;

IF iInitParam == 2 THEN
	iInitParam = 0;
ENDIF;
